\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{testlib_8h_source_l00676}00676\ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{testlib_8h_source_l00677}00677\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Very\ simple\ regex-\/like\ pattern.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{testlib_8h_source_l00678}00678\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ It\ used\ for\ two\ purposes:\ validation\ and\ generation.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{testlib_8h_source_l00679}00679\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{testlib_8h_source_l00680}00680\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ For\ example,\ pattern("{}[a-\/z]\{1,5\}"{}).next(rnd)\ will\ return}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{testlib_8h_source_l00681}00681\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ random\ string\ from\ lowercase\ latin\ letters\ with\ length}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{testlib_8h_source_l00682}00682\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ from\ 1\ to\ 5.\ It\ is\ easier\ to\ call\ rnd.next("{}[a-\/z]\{1,5\}"{})}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{testlib_8h_source_l00683}00683\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ for\ the\ same\ effect.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{testlib_8h_source_l00684}00684\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{testlib_8h_source_l00685}00685\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Another\ samples:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{testlib_8h_source_l00686}00686\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ "{}mike|john"{}\ will\ generate\ (match)\ "{}mike"{}\ or\ "{}john"{};}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{testlib_8h_source_l00687}00687\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ "{}-\/?[1-\/9][0-\/9]\{0,3\}"{}\ will\ generate\ (match)\ non-\/zero\ integers\ from\ -\/9999\ to\ 9999;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{testlib_8h_source_l00688}00688\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ "{}id-\/([ac]|b\{2\})"{}\ will\ generate\ (match)\ "{}id-\/a"{},\ "{}id-\/bb"{},\ "{}id-\/c"{};}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{testlib_8h_source_l00689}00689\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ "{}[\string^0-\/9]*"{}\ will\ match\ sequences\ (empty\ or\ non-\/empty)\ without\ digits,\ you\ can't}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{testlib_8h_source_l00690}00690\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ use\ it\ for\ generations.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{testlib_8h_source_l00691}00691\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{testlib_8h_source_l00692}00692\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ You\ can't\ use\ pattern\ for\ generation\ if\ it\ contains\ meta-\/symbol\ '*'.\ Also\ it}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{testlib_8h_source_l00693}00693\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ is\ not\ recommended\ to\ use\ it\ for\ char-\/sets\ with\ meta-\/symbol\ '\string^'\ like\ [\string^a-\/z].}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{testlib_8h_source_l00694}00694\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{testlib_8h_source_l00695}00695\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ For\ matching\ very\ simple\ greedy\ algorithm\ is\ used.\ For\ example,\ pattern}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{testlib_8h_source_l00696}00696\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ "{}[0-\/9]?1"{}\ will\ not\ match\ "{}1"{},\ because\ of\ greedy\ nature\ of\ matching.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{testlib_8h_source_l00697}00697\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Alternations\ (meta-\/symbols\ "{}|"{})\ are\ processed\ with\ brute-\/force\ algorithm,\ so}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{testlib_8h_source_l00698}00698\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ do\ not\ use\ many\ alternations\ in\ one\ expression.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{testlib_8h_source_l00699}00699\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{testlib_8h_source_l00700}00700\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ If\ you\ want\ to\ use\ one\ expression\ many\ times\ it\ is\ better\ to\ compile\ it\ into}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{testlib_8h_source_l00701}00701\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ a\ single\ pattern\ like\ "{}pattern\ p("{}[a-\/z]+"{})"{}.\ Later\ you\ can\ use}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{testlib_8h_source_l00702}00702\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ "{}p.matches(std::string\ s)"{}\ or\ "{}p.next(random\_t\&\ rd)"{}\ to\ check\ matching\ or\ generate}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{testlib_8h_source_l00703}00703\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ new\ string\ by\ pattern.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{testlib_8h_source_l00704}00704\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{testlib_8h_source_l00705}00705\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Simpler\ way\ to\ read\ token\ and\ check\ it\ for\ pattern\ matching\ is\ "{}inf.readToken("{}[a-\/z]+"{})"{}.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{testlib_8h_source_l00706}00706\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{testlib_8h_source_l00707}00707\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ All\ spaces\ are\ ignored\ in\ regex,\ unless\ escaped\ with\ \(\backslash\).\ For\ example,\ ouf.readLine("{}NO\ SOLUTION"{})}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{testlib_8h_source_l00708}00708\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ will\ expect\ "{}NOSOLUTION"{},\ the\ correct\ call\ should\ be\ ouf.readLine("{}NO\(\backslash\)\(\backslash\)\ SOLUTION"{})\ or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{testlib_8h_source_l00709}00709\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ ouf.readLine(R"{}(NO\(\backslash\)\ SOLUTION)"{})\ if\ you\ prefer\ raw\ string\ literals\ from\ C++11.}}
